def get_model():
    print('Build model ...')
    text_input = Input(shape=(Padding_Length, ), name='text_input')
    #overall_feature_input = Input(shape=(num_feature,), name='overall_feature_input')
    sentence_feature_input = Input(shape=(max_sent_length, 2,), name='sentence_feature_input')
    # print(text_input) # Tensor("text_input:0", shape=(?, 4472), dtype=float32)
    # print(overall_feature_input)
    print(sentence_feature_input)

    embedding_layer = Embedding(input_dim=len(word_index) + 1,
                                output_dim=100,
                                weights=[embeddings_matrix],
                                input_length=Padding_Length,
                                trainable=False,
                                mask_zero=True)
    embedding = embedding_layer(text_input)  # tensor (?, 4472, 100)
    lstm1 = LSTM(64, return_sequences=True)(embedding)  # (?, ?, 64)

    a = [i for i in range(85, 4472, 86)]
    sent_layer = [Lambda(lambda t: t[:, i, :])(lstm1) for i in a]
    sent_output = Lambda(stack)(sent_layer)
    print(sent_output)  # (?, 52, 64)
    sent_feature_concat_layer = Lambda(concatenate)([sent_output, sentence_feature_input])
    lstm2 = LSTM(32)(sent_feature_concat_layer)
    # dense1 = Dense(128, activation='relu')(lstm)
    # print(lstm2)¡¡# (?, 32)


    #concat_layer = Lambda(concatenate)([lstm2, overall_feature_input])

    #dense1 = Dense(32, activation='sigmoid')(concat_layer)
    #dense2 = Dense(32, activation='relu')(dense1)
    output = Dense(1, activation='relu')(lstm2)
    model = Model(inputs=[text_input, sentence_feature_input], outputs=output)
    model.summary()
    return model
